Let \mu be the following measure on \omega_3:
A has \mu-measure one iff there is a club C in \omega_1 such that for any function
	f : \omega_1^3 ---> C 
with the property that for a club E in \omega_1, for any a>b>c in E, for any a'>b'>c' in E, 
	f(a,c,b) > f(a',c',b') iff (a,c,b)>(a',c',b') in the lexicograpich order
the ordinal represented modulo (club measure on \omega_1)^2 by the function
	(a,c) |---> \sup_{b<a} f(a,c,b)
belongs A.

Then j^\mu \circ j^\mu is equal to a single ultrapower map induced by the following level-2 tree of cardinality 6051.
